66	Welcome to FiftyOne!
67	
68	This quickstart downloaded a dataset from the Dataset Zoo and created a
69	session, which is a connection to an instance of the App.
70	
71	The dataset contains ground truth labels in a `ground_truth` field and
72	predictions from an off-the-shelf detector in a `predictions` field. It also
73	has a `uniqueness` field that indexes the dataset by visual uniqueness.
74	
75	Here are some things you can do to explore the dataset:
76	
77	
78	(a) Click on an image to explore its labels in more detail
79	
80	
81	(b) Sort the dataset by uniqueness:
82	
83	    - Click `add stage`
84	    - Select the `SortBy` stage
85	    - Select the `uniqueness` field
86	
87	    Try setting `reverse` to `True` to show the *most unique* images first.
88	    Try setting `reverse` to `False` to show the *least unique* images first.
89	
90	
91	(c) Filter predictions by confidence
92	
93	    The predictions field is noisy, but you can use FiftyOne to filter them!
94	
95	    In the filters menu on the left, click on the `v` caret to the
96	    right of the `predictions` field to open a label filter. Drag the
97	    confidence slider to only include predictions with confidence at least 0.8!
98	
99	    You can also filter the detections from Python. Assuming you ran the
100	    quickstart like this::
101	
102	        import fiftyone as fo
103	
104	        dataset, session = fo.quickstart()
105	
106	    Then you can filter the predictions by creating a view:
107	
108	        from fiftyone import ViewField as F
109	
110	        # Create a view that only contains predictions whose confidence is at
111	        # least 0.8
112	        high_conf_view = dataset.filter_labels("predictions", F("confidence") > 0.8)
113	
114	        # Open the view in the App!

116	
117	Resources:
118
